                        <div data-reactid="456">
                         My place is the perfect place to stay when visiting Los Angeles, West Hollywood, or Beverly Hills. It is a perfect location close to many restaurants, shopping and sights. Private patio behind and interior has large flat screen TV with fast Wifi!
                        </div>
                        <div data-reactid="457">
                         Welcome to my apartment! Let me tell you a bit about my home and the neighborhood. My home is a one bedroom house that has been recently renovated. If you rent the apartment, it is private rental of the entire apartment, so no one stays there with you. All of the furniture is in excellent condition and all of the linens and towels are new and fresh. The apartment has a great TV area with a couch, coffee table and chair and a large high definition TV that is connected to the free WiFi internet in the house. The WiFi is high speed and the TV has free Netflix and Hulu to watch. There is also a kitchen which is open to a dining room / kitchen table for 4 people. The bedroom is very spacious and has a huge closet. The apartment also has a great PRIVATE patio behind the apartment under the trees with a wood seating area and table for 4 people. The apartment gets tons of light and the patio is great for having a morning coffee in the California Sunshine. The neighborhood is also great. My apartment is located in the best location in Los Angeles, it is on the border of Beverly Hills and West Hollywood. There are many places to walk from my apartment but it's also very centrally located in LA: LAX Airport: 20 minutes by car The Grove: 5 minutes by car Santa Monica Pier: 20 minutes by car Hollywood Walk of Fame: 10 minutes by car Venice Boardwalk: 30 minutes by car The area has many things to do, from the best restaurants to the best shopping and sightseeing. It is also in the center of LA so it is easy to get around to different places. So many great places to walk to including coffee shops and museums. The apartment is also located next to Cedars Sinai Hospital. Although you probably have heard and know all about Beverly Hills, here is a bit about the WeHo which might be useful. "When it comes to style, design, and decor, West Hollywood, or WeHo, ranks highly. WeHo means being just off of Melrose and walking distance to all shops/restaurants on Beverly, La Cienega, Fairfax, Melrose, Farmer's Market, The Grove and the Beverly Center. Walk the Sunset Strip and wander Melrose District by day. Twirl, sip, and swirl by night—WeHo is a 24/7 destination. The Sunset Strip and Sunset Plaza remain entertainment destinations for locals and visitors looking for stylish respites in an urban setting. Bookstores, art galleries, yoga studios, and cross-fit bootcamps line up along the Sunset Strip. Bars, lounges, music venues, comedy clubs, and performance galleries invite nighttime walkers, gawkers and dancers. The location is perfect with tons of shopping, restaurant, bars, galleries, and hiking within minutes of walking or by car. Renowned for its shopping, dining, and entertainment options, Melrose District doesn't disappoint. The parade of boutiques, eateries, and venues begins at WeHo's border with Beverly Hills and stretches all the way to Silver Lake, another LA favorite for hip exploration. Home to Pacific Design Center and Museum of Contemporary Art, LA Pacific Design Center, WeHo promotes conscientious creation and spatial shaping."
                        </div>

There's also a creepy painting that says "God Is A Feeling" in the dining room that looks like it was plucked off the wall from the Bates Motel and put in the apartment. That said, check in was pretty easy and the location isn't bad. I wouldn't say you should avoid this listing at all costs, but I know I'm not likely to come back.</p><span data-reactid="2118">Colton</span><span data-reactid="2119">2017-02-20T00:00:00Z</span></li>

                        <div data-reactid="2213">
                         This classy 1 bedroom and 1 bathroom apartment with a spacious living room, located in West Los Angeles, is perfect for anyone looking to make the most out of Los Angeles and all its tourist attractions. It has a separate dining area next to the kitchen and a couch in the living room that can easily be turned into a bed. With free high speed internet and one compact parking spot, this place has something for everyone. Pet and smoking friendly! An upscale and urban area neighboring Beverly Hills and West Hollywood, there is so much to do around the area, especially if you want to make the most of Los Angeles and everything that the city has to offer. Los Angeles and it’s amazing sunny weather makes it perfect for everyday beach day! Head on to Santa Monica, drive down the Pacific Coast Highway (PCH) and head towards Malibu or go to Venice beach and walk the boardwalk, all within a driving distance of 20-30 minutes. Or if you’re looking to try out some of the amazing cuisines, just head on over to Beverly Hills and choose from fine dining to chilling at a local cafe, the options are endless. Make your way to Rodeo drive and check out all the designer boutiques and have lunch or dinner at one of the chic restaurants. If you’re looking to visit some museums, the Ace Gallery in Beverly Hills, that exhibits work of emerging artists alongside established artists. Location is key when you want to make the most of Los Angeles and this apartment is perfect for that along with the comfortable living.
